## 104. Sep 19, 2025 Â· 4:54 AM UTC Â· 1968901491877691662#m

> 7ï¸âƒ£ Risk Controls

> â€¢ Boosted yield distribution
> Think of vePENDLE as the long-term incentive + governance backbone.
>  
> ðŸ”¹ PendleSwap
> A one-stop swap interface.
> â€¢ Swap between PT/YT & underlying assets
> â€¢ Functions as a DEX aggregator
> â€¢ Increases composability & convenience
> Not a new primitive â€” but makes Pendle way easier to use.
>  
> ðŸ”¹ Points Market
> Yes, even points get a market.
> â€¢ Trade project loyalty/airdrop points early
> â€¢ Arbitrage points valuations
> â€¢ Speculative, narrative-driven use case
> Less about core value, more about capturing hype & flows.
>  
> TL;DR Extra Features ðŸ‘‡
> â€¢ vePENDLE â†’ align incentives + boost yields
> â€¢ PendleSwap â†’ smooth UX for PT/YT <-> underlying
> â€¢ Points Market â†’ speculative edge for airdrop hunters

## 139. Sep 16, 2025 Â· 2:56 PM UTC Â· 1967965788805173577#m
- é“¾æŽ¥ï¼šhttps://twitter.com/0xjacobzhao/status/1967965788805173577#m
- ä½œè€…ï¼š@0xjacobzhao

> 4/
> Beyond PT/YT, @pendle_fi  launched @boros_fi  â€” a funding rate trading module. It turns funding rates (usually a cost of perps) into a tokenized, tradable instrument. Core primitive: Yield Units (YU) ðŸ‘‡
> ðŸ‘‰ Like importing Interest Rate Swaps (IRS) & basis trades into DeFi.
>  
> ðŸŽ¯ Speculation
> Bet directly on funding rate direction:
> â€¢ Long YU = pay fixed, receive floating â†’ bullish on funding â†‘
> â€¢ Short YU = receive fixed, pay floating â†’ bearish on funding â†“
> ðŸ‘‰ TradFi analogy: payer/receiver swaps.
>  
> ðŸ›¡ï¸ Hedging
> For whales & institutions with big perp books:
> â€¢ Funding Cost Hedge: Long Perp + Long YU â†’ lock floating cost into fixed
> â€¢ Funding Income Hedge: Short Perp + Short YU â†’ lock floating income into fixed
> = Smooth PnL, no more funding volatility.
>  
> âš–ï¸ Arbitrage
> Delta-neutral yield plays & spread trades:
> â€¢ Stake stETH (~4% yield) + Short Perp + Short YU â†’ stable carry
> â€¢ Cross-Market Arb: Futures Premium vs Boros APR â†’ long cheap, short rich
> â€¢ Term Arb: long cheap maturity YU, short expensive maturity YU
> ðŸ‘‰ Like gov bond yield curve arb, but in DeFi.
>  
> Boros = DeFiâ€™s interest rate derivatives market
> â€¢ Speculation â†’ directional rate bets
> â€¢ Hedging â†’ lock perp costs/income
> â€¢ Arbitrage â†’ harvest spreads across markets & maturities
> âš ï¸ Best suited for pro capital & institutions, less retail friendly.

## 140. Sep 16, 2025 Â· 2:45 PM UTC Â· 1967962974649454834#m
- é“¾æŽ¥ï¼šhttps://twitter.com/0xjacobzhao/status/1967962974649454834#m
- ä½œè€…ï¼š@0xjacobzhao

> 3/
> @pendle_fi  PT/YT design unlocks 4 major strategy paths, each matching different risk appetites:
>  
> ðŸ”¹ Fixed Income (PT Strategy)
> Buy PT (Principal Token) at a discount â†’ redeem 1:1 at maturity.
> Effectively an on-chain zero-coupon bond.
> Lock in fixed yield, no surprises.
> âœ… Best for conservative investors
> âš ï¸ Risk: opportunity cost if yields rise elsewhere.
>  
> ðŸ”¹ Yield Speculation (YT Strategy)
> Buy YT (Yield Token) â†’ entitled to all yield until maturity.
> YT = a pure play on future yields.
> If staking APR or lending rates rise, YT appreciates.
> If yields collapse â†’ YT can trend toward 0.
> âœ… High-risk, high-reward.
> âš ï¸ Requires strong views on rate trends.
>  
> ðŸ”¹ Curve Arbitrage
> PT & YT have maturities (e.g., 1M, 3M, 6M).
> Sometimes mispricings occur across different tenors.
> Arbitrage = long undervalued PT/YT, short overvalued one â†’ capture spread.
> âœ… Market-neutral strategy
> âš ï¸ Requires active monitoring + execution skill.
>  
> ðŸ”¹ Leveraged Yield
> Use PT or YT as collateral in lending protocols.
> Borrow stables or ETH â†’ loop back into PT or YT positions.
> Goal: amplify returns by stacking exposure.
> âœ… Boosts APY significantly
> âš ï¸ Adds liquidation & smart contract risk

> âœ…System Impact
> Treasuries: Interlinked w/ TradFi (Fed policy, stock liquidity).
> Luna: Closed crypto loop. No external stabilizers.
>  
> âœ…Endgame
> Treasuries: Worst case = stock crash + BTC sell pressure â†’ more volatility, assets still exist.
> Luna: Worst case = total wipeout.
>  
> Bottom Line: Treasuries â‰  Luna, They are bridges to TradFi and compliance. But in downturns, they flip from capital gateways â†’ volatility amplifiers.

## 162. Sep 9, 2025 Â· 10:16 AM UTC Â· 1965358525330395486#m
- é“¾æŽ¥ï¼šhttps://twitter.com/0xjacobzhao/status/1965358525330395486#m
- ä½œè€…ï¼š@0xjacobzhao

> 3/ Treasury selloffs in downturns â€“ whatâ€™s the risk?
>  
> mNAV = Enterprise Value Ã· Net Asset Value
> EV = market cap + debt + preferred stock â€“ cash
> NAV = value of crypto holdings at current prices
> This ratio = the heartbeat of every treasury company.
>  
> When mNAV > 1 (premium):
> Market pays for growth, brand, financing ability â†’ Company issues shares â†’ raises cash â†’ buys BTC/ETH â†’ Buying pressure lifts BTC â†’ NAV grows â†’ stock rises
> ðŸ‘‰ The Asset Expansion Flywheel (see: MicroStrategy).
>  
> When mNAV < 1 (discount):
> Market questions valuation â†’ Stock falls â†’ investors sell harder â†’ Company may dump BTC/ETH to defend ratio â†’ Selling drives BTC lower â†’ NAV shrinks â†’ stock falls more
> ðŸ‘‰ Thatâ€™s the path to a death spiral.
>  
> This looks like a balance-sheet recession in TradFiâ€”
> but in crypto it plays out faster and sharper.
> Some firms may try share buybacks (raise BTC per share), but not all have that option.

> Type 1: Full equivalence â†’ lowest migration, slow proofs (ex: @taikoxyz)
> Type 2: Full compatibility â†’ minimal changes (ex: @Scroll_ZKP @LineaBuild)
> Type 2.5: Semi-compat â†’ tweak gas/ops (ex: @0xPolygon zkEVM, @KakarotZkEvm)
> Type 3: Partial compat â†’ runs most apps, infra gaps (ex: @zksync Era)
> Type 4: Language-level â†’ compile from high-level (ex: @StarknetFndn Cairo)
>  
> Main theme = zkRollup wars.
> Problems:
> 1âƒ£ EVM circuits = hard, inefficient
> 2âƒ£ ZK potential goes far beyond scaling
